Northeast Anti-Japanese Army Bloody Battle at Xilin River

Japanese Troops in Northern Manchuria Restrained by Soviet Russia

Japanese Troops Retreat in Battle of Xilin River

Harbin Correspondence: Recently, the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army has been actively preparing for war with Japanese and Russian troops in northern Manchuria. The majority of Japanese and puppet troops have been transferred to important locations such as Manzhouli and Hailun, believing that there is an opportunity to take advantage. After occupying Sandangang on the 3rd of this month, the Japanese troops were quite alarmed. At the same time, due to the increasingly serious military situation in northern Manchuria, they did not take an offensive stance against the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army, but only defended. On the 7th of this month, the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army convened a meeting of military officers and decided to take the opportunity to advance along the Chinese Eastern Railway. It is also reported that the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army recently purchased five fighter planes from a certain country. The pilots are said to be Russian, and the planes provide cover during combat. Moreover, the organization and training of the troops are more effective than those of the former Northeast Army, and they have greater combat capabilities. The Japanese and puppet troops feel quite uneasy. On the 8th of this month, the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army attacked Xilin River Station. They made contact with the Japanese army about 50 miles from the station. Both sides charged and engaged in close combat, fighting fiercely for a day and night. The morale of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army grew stronger. They used heavy artillery to cover the attack. At about 9:00 PM that night, they secretly entered the Japanese army's defenses. The Japanese army's defenses were slightly weaker at night, so they scattered in confusion and were in a very embarrassing situation. As a result, more than 40 Japanese soldiers were killed, and the defense line was completely broken. On the morning of the 10th, the Japanese troops retreated to Maqiaohe and urgently telegraphed the Changchun Command for reinforcements. It is reported that the number of troops in the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army has now reached more than 80,000. (Northeast Agency)

Japanese Planes Suddenly Fly Over Zhangjiakou

Zhao Dengyu's Division Enters Guyuan

Japan Forces Song's Troops to Withdraw from Eastern Chahar

Special Dispatch from Beiping: Zhao Dengyu's division of Song Zheyuan's 29th Army, due to bandit disturbances in the Guyuan area (more than ten li outside Dushikou), causing hardship for the people, and in order to maintain law and order, dispatched troops to the vicinity of Guyuan city on the morning of the 13th. The puppet army of Li Shouxin immediately retreated north. On the 14th, Zhao's troops entered Guyuan. Prior to this, He Yingqin, acting chairman of the Beiping Military Branch, had met with Shibayama, the military attaché of the Japanese embassy, to explain the situation, stating that the Chahar provincial army intended to enter Guyuan to suppress bandits but would not advance further north, requesting their understanding. Shibayama replied that the Chinese government had the right to deal with the bandits in Chahar Province, and he would inform the Kwantung Army of the matter. However, as soon as Zhao's division arrived in Guyuan, Japanese planes flew from the southeast to the sky above Zhangjiakou, circling for more than twenty minutes and dropping many leaflets with absurd wording. Among them was a so-called warning letter, the full text of which is as follows: (According to the provisions of the Sino-Japanese Truce Agreement, the extension line of Changping and Yanqing, that is, the area east of Longguan and Zhangbei, is where Chinese troops should not enter without authorization, as this is a clear violation of the agreement. Recently, it has been heard that Song Zheyuan's troops have successively entered the area east of this line without regard for the spirit of the truce agreement. It is hoped that said troops will change their attitude and quickly withdraw their infantry to the west of the Changping-Yanqing-Longguan-Zhangbei line. Otherwise, the Japanese (Manchukuo) armies, in order to maintain the spirit of the truce agreement, will inevitably take decisive measures, not only attacking said troops, but also bombing Zhangjiakou, the source of their strategy. Should other important relations arise as a result, the responsibility for this will rest entirely with Song Zheyuan's army. This needs no further explanation. This is a special declaration and warning, Kwantung Army Resident Officer in Chengde, Matsumuro Takayoshi.) The Japanese planes then flew towards Chengde. Song Zheyuan, chairman of the Chahar provincial government, went to Tianjin to visit his family a few days ago. After receiving a report from the Chahar provincial government, he took the Beining train to Beiping on the evening of the 15th. According to Song, he went to Tianjin to visit his family and was not very familiar with the Japanese planes reconnaissance of Zhangjiakou. The bandit army of Li Shouxin in Duolun and Guyuan harassed the local area, and everyone should punish them. Zhao Dengyu's division implemented suppression in order to maintain law and order and purely to pacify the people, with no other intention. He just heard Qin (Dechun), the chief of staff, report that the Japanese planes intended to bomb Zhangjiakou, and this matter should be negotiated with the Japanese side by the government. He himself would visit Chairman He on the 16th and return to Chahar on the 18th. If necessary, he could also depart earlier. After He Yingqin received a report from Yang Zhennan, the secretary-general of the Chahar provincial government, he summoned Qin Dechun, the director of the Chahar Civil Affairs Department, and Xiong Bin, etc., around 4 p.m. on the 15th to discuss the matter. In addition to preparing to lodge a protest with the Japanese side, in order to avoid the situation escalating, he had telegraphed Zhao Dengyu's division to stop in Guyuan and await orders. At the same time, he ordered Yin Tong, a receiving commissioner, to negotiate with Yano Shin, the acting representative of the Japanese Embassy in China, and Lieutenant Colonel Shibayama, the military attaché of the Japanese Embassy. Yin Jing went to the Japanese Embassy to visit Shibayama to inquire about the truth and asked the Kwantung Army to find a way to prevent sending planes to Zhangjiakou again. Shibayama promised to forward our views to the Kwantung Army and Matsumuro. Yano Shin, the Japanese acting representative, also visited Chairman He on the 16th at 11 a.m. at Jurentang, accompanied by Harada Ryuichi, a Chinese counselor, explaining that Japan had no intention of expanding the situation. The reason why Matsumuro sent planes to Zhangjiakou to distribute leaflets was probably to prevent Song's troops from intending to advance east. Chairman He then explained again that our side had already notified them of the bandit suppression in advance, and Yano then withdrew.

At present, in eastern Chahar, Zhao Dengyu's troops have already entered Guyuan, and the local troops of Li Shouxin and Suo Huachen, and more than a thousand miscellaneous troops, have retreated to Duolun. Yao Jingchuan is responsible for guarding Baochang, and Ruan Xuanwu is responsible for guarding Kangbao, to prevent miscellaneous troops and puppet troops from disturbing the west. Song Zheyuan previously believed that the security of the Zhangjiakou area was very important, so he appointed Feng Zhi'an, commander of the 37th Division, as the garrison commander of Zhangjiakou. There are three reasons for the Japanese provocation this time: (1) After the Japanese clique forcibly occupied Rehe, it publicly declared its intention to划師 (劃歸) Chahar Province into the puppet (Manchukuo) state. Our anti-Japanese troops are now going to northern Chahar to take over defense, and the Japanese side will definitely oppose this. (2) In order to achieve its ambition to annex North China, the Japanese clique is buying traitors everywhere in our territory and recruiting bandit troops. The puppet troops and bandits in eastern Hebei and northern Hebei have already refused our country's suppression. The Japanese army will also maintain and protect the puppet troops of Li Shouxin in eastern Chahar, so that they can be used in the future. (3) The Japanese side is afraid that Song's troops will advance north from Guyuan again and recapture Duolun, so it is using this intimidating method. (16th)

Japanese Army Refuses to Suppress Bandits in Eastern Luan

Only Allows Us to Increase Security Forces for Vigilance

Japanese Troops Greatly Increased at Various Passes of the Great Wall

Japanese Army in Yu Forcing People to Recognize the Puppet State

Dispatch from Beiping: Bandits in eastern Luan are rampant. Our side believes that a small number of security forces cannot eliminate them, and has sent personnel to contact Shibayama, the military attaché of the Japanese embassy, and Nakamura, the commander of the Tianjin garrison, to discuss sending troops to suppress them, but to no avail. Therefore, a few days ago, the Receiving Committee sent personnel to Changchun to meet with Hishikari Takashi, commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army, to discuss the matter and negotiate the return of various passes of the Great Wall. The personnel sent a telegram to Beiping today (16th), stating that the Kwantung Army, under the pretext of the truce agreement, refused our side to send troops to the war zone to suppress bandits and only allowed increasing security forces to engage in vigilance. After receiving the telegram, the authorities immediately ordered the personnel to continue negotiations and stepped up the training of security forces. If sending troops to suppress bandits is completely hopeless, they will decide to increase the deployment of security forces to carry out suppression and maintain local peace, and relieve the people from distress. The Japanese side is using the bandits in the war zone and does not want our side to eliminate them. At the same time, major passes of the Great Wall are guarded by Japanese troops. Before they are returned, bandits can enter from outside each pass in an endless stream. Even if we want to eliminate them, it is difficult to do so in reality. In recent days, in the Jianchangying area within Lengkou, more than 600 Japanese soldiers have arrived from Yu. Saheqiao inside Xifengkou has also increased by 300 to 400 soldiers and built a large-scale airfield there. The Japanese army's various deployments at the passes are preparing to stay for a long time, and it is feared that negotiations for return are impossible. As for Shanhaiguan, after repeated negotiations to restore the pre-war state, the Japanese side has ignored them. Recently, they have intensified their efforts to force the people of Yu and Guan to elect representatives to go to Changchun to petition for劃歸 (劃歸) Yu and Guan to the puppet state. Each elected representative was given 100 yuan for travel expenses. Yesterday (15th), the Japanese held an anniversary celebration of Japan's recognition of the puppet state in Yu and Guan, and sent police to force shops and households in the city and countryside to hang the puppet state's flag and paste absurd slogans everywhere. Under the oppression, the people dared to be angry but dared not speak out. (September 16)

Chiang Kai-shek's Instruction on the Significance of Blocking Bandit Areas

Blocking Bandit Areas is an Effective Method of Controlling Bandits

Designates Eight Zones and Dispatches Commissioners for Supervision

Dispatch from Nanchang: Chiang Kai-shek believes that blocking bandit areas and cutting off bandit supplies is an effective method of controlling bandits. The general public inevitably complains about various restrictions on the transportation, hoarding, and purchase of goods, showing a lack of understanding of the purpose of implementing the blockade policy. In order to instruct officials and civilians to temporarily endure small pains for the sake of long-term peace, a proclamation is issued to all provinces for their information. The proclamation says: (In recent years, the Red Bandits, like petty villains, have run rampant north and south of the Yangtze River. Although the National Army has repeatedly suppressed them, it has not yet achieved the effect of annihilating them. The reason for this is that the country has many troubles, and military and political affairs have not been able to focus their efforts, leading to a prairie fire. Furthermore, unscrupulous people in various places have either provided material assistance to the bandits or acted as spies to help the bandits, which is the biggest reason for the bandits' rampant activities. The Committee Chairman is ordered to supervise the suppression and clear them out within a time limit. It is believed that rectifying the military ranks and improving politics are the fundamental goals of suppressing bandits, while intensifying the blockade and cutting off supplies are effective methods of controlling bandits. Therefore, in May of this year, the measures for blocking bandit areas were formulated and promulgated for implementation. However, reports have been received from various parties that the general public inevitably complains about various restrictions on the transportation, hoarding, and purchase of goods, showing a lack of understanding of the purpose of implementing the blockade policy. It must be known that the Red Bandits are more venomous than snakes and scorpions, turning every village they pass into ruins and every county they capture into desolation. If they are still allowed to spread, the small result will be that one place will be ravaged, and the large result will be that the entire nation and country will fall into a terrible state of no return. The facts are all there, and who does not gnash their teeth? At this time when the army is encircling and suppressing them, if we do not fortify our walls and clear the fields, so that the bandits have nothing to plunder when they advance and nothing to eat when they retreat, how can we quickly annihilate the evil and secure our people? As the saying goes, "If a poisonous snake bites the hand, a brave man will cut off his wrist." The people of each place have lived off the land for many years and have long had sympathy for loving their homeland and defending the country. Since they earnestly desire governance, they should all promote the strictness of the blockade, quickly pacify the bandit lair, and ascend to peace together. Isn't that very good? After this earnest exhortation, it is deeply hoped that everyone will understand this intention, endure temporary small pains, and plan for long-term peace. If there are unscrupulous officials, or district and baojia heads, who falsely use the name of blockade and public sale to secretly extort money and deceive property, once the people report the facts, the Committee Chairman will severely punish them according to the law and will never tolerate them. Everyone must abide by this and keep it in mind.)

Chiang Kai-shek designated eight zones for blocking bandit areas and appointed Xia Tongshou as the supervisor of the first zone, covering five counties including Shangrao; Ren Jinzhang as the supervisor of the second zone, covering counties including Dongxiang; Shi Guangying as the supervisor of the third zone, covering five counties including Wannian; He Guanglie as the supervisor of the fourth zone, covering five counties including Linchuan; He Kunxiong as the supervisor of the fifth zone, covering five counties including Fengcheng; Zhu Yiming as the supervisor of the sixth zone, covering five counties including Ji'an; Mei E as the supervisor of the seventh zone, covering five counties including Qingjiang; and Hong Lu as the supervisor of the eighth zone, covering five counties including Xiushui, to supervise the counties and strictly block them. In order to understand the true situation of the blockade in each county and examine the work of the supervisors in each county, Chiang Kai-shek specially dispatched Song Canru, a staff member with the rank of colonel in the General Headquarters, to inspect the eastern zone, and Peng Bingchu, a staff member with the rank of colonel, to inspect the western zone. After receiving the orders, each officer went to each county a few days ago to conduct strict assessments and provide instructions on everything. (September 15, Datong News Agency)

National Army Suppresses Bandits on Three Routes on the Border of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui

Liu Zhenhua Requests the Designation of a Special Zone

He Chengjun Goes to Lushan to Request Instructions on Post-War Affairs

Dispatch from Hankou: Since Liu Zhenhua, as supervisor of troops, advanced to suppress remaining bandits on the border of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, there have been more than twenty battles, large and small. Four to five thousand bandits have been captured and beheaded successively. Many weapons such as rifles, machine guns, knives, and spears have been seized. The only Lie Ning No. 1 aircraft was also captured. However, the bandits' pseudo-25th Army and pseudo-Independent Division, which are known as elite, still have more than 10,000 troops and 4,000 to 5,000 guns, with Tangjiahui as their main lair, attempting to counterattack. When Liu Zhenhua heard the report, he sent troops on three routes on the 13th to suppress them. One route was Song Tiancai's division, one route was Hao Mengling's division, and Liu's own 64th division was also responsible for one route, converging and advancing. On the 14th, Song led the two brigades of Shi Guangqin and Lu Tianfu to advance from Sunjiadian towards Wamiaoji, contacting the main force of the bandits. After four hours of fighting, they finally occupied Wamiaoji and successively recovered the key points of Sidaohe, Gaojiachong, and Chenjiashan. Because the National Army directly attacked Tangjiahui's lair, the bandits were deeply afraid of being attacked from both sides and hurriedly fled back to Tangjiahui, while dividing their troops to defend Dafoshan, to resist Song's division. It is reported that the National Army on all routes has established contact and will launch a general suppression on the 15th, with a deadline to recover. If this force is annihilated, other sporadic bandits can be easily solved.

As for the post-war issues in the border area, the first stage is to take in refugees and provide emergency relief. The provincial governments of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui have each allocated 20,000 yuan. Hubei sent Lei Bingkun, and Anhui sent Hou Huaiyuan, to depart with the army and handle relief affairs. Henan requested that the Border Area Headquarters distribute the funds on its behalf. Seven refugee shelters have been established one after another, with Henan setting up shelters in Guangshan, Shangcheng, Jingfu, and Zhoujiafan; Hubei setting up shelters in Huang'an and Macheng; and Anhui setting up a shelter in Lihuang. More than 20,000 refugees have now been taken in. However, Liu Zhenhua believed that the relief funds were too small to be distributed, and proposed a discussion at the Huangchuan meeting, which decided that the total amount of post-war reconstruction funds would be 4.9 million yuan, with 1 million yuan continuing to be used for relief and 3.9 million yuan being used for rural reconstruction. He had previously telegraphed Chiang Kai-shek, requesting approval and issuance. After receiving the telegram, Chiang decided to forward it to the central government for allocation together with the post-war reconstruction case in Jiangxi, and first remitted 100,000 yuan for Liu to use. As for activating finance, he considered the urgency and asked Liu to write to the Farmers Banks of the four provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi, asking them to establish branches in Lu'an County, Anhui Province, and to the Hubei Provincial Government, ordering the Provincial Bank to establish a branch in Huang'an, as the hub of economic penetration in the area. In addition, what should be noted is the suggestion to Chiang Kai-shek to designate the border area of the three provinces as a special administrative region. On the 15th, He Chengjun went to Lushan upon Chiang's summons to request instructions on post-war measures. Provincial Committee member Li Shucheng accompanied him, bearing the task of reporting to Chiang and requesting the designation of a special administrative region. Li had attended the Huangchuan meeting on behalf of the Hubei Provincial Government and was elected as the representative to Lushan. (September 16)

Yellow River Flooding in Ningxia

Tens of Breaches in Jinji, Zhongwei, and Other Counties

More Than a Thousand Villages Washed Away, Nearly a Million Starving People

Ningxia is located in the upper reaches of the Yellow River. In past years, floods harmed the lower reaches, and Gansu and Ningxia were spared. This year's flood season was unusually severe in the three provinces of Henan, Shandong, and Jiangsu. Unexpectedly, after autumn, Ningxia experienced mountain torrents, and the Yellow River was also surging and overflowing. The irrigation canals in Ningxia are higher than the flat ground, so once a breach occurs, it cannot be contained. Currently, there are dozens of breaches in the counties along the river, such as Zhongwei, Jinji, Lingwu, and Dengkou. The villages along the river are covered in water, especially in Jinji and Zhongwei. It is estimated that more than a thousand villages have been washed away, and there are nearly a million starving people. The weather in the northern frontier is colder than in the Central Plains, and the disaster victims are suffering from hunger and cold, with no homes to return to. The situation is extremely tragic. It is reported that the Ningxia Province has sent provincial committee member Hai Tao to request relief from the central government.

Wujiang Tongren Pawnshop Scheduled to Pay Compensation

The Tongren Pawnshop in this county caught fire on April 12, resulting in the destruction of the entire pawnshop. Local gentry and local agencies organized a Tongren Pawnshop Fire Disaster Relief Committee to discuss compensation methods, which were submitted to the county government for transfer to the Construction and Civil Affairs Departments for approval. After receiving approval, the committee convened a second committee meeting, chaired by Zhu Yuanzhi. (1) It was resolved that the compensation period would begin on October 12 and end in three months. (2) It was resolved that the location would still be at the original site of the Tongren Pawnshop in NanDai, Tongli. (3) It was resolved to elect Fan Kuichen, Pang Qinsheng, Zhou Shihong, Wang Shaobo, Wang Yiting, Wang Dehui, and others as members of the compensation supervision committee. (4) It was resolved to submit a request to the county to unseal the dug-up pawned goods for liquidation and compensation. (5) It was resolved that the pawned goods submitted by Committee Member Yang Zichun for 30% compensation as resolved in the previous meeting should be reduced by half the interest according to the ticket to show consideration for the pawn clients.

Murderer in North 㘮 Executed

Zhan Mao, from North 㘮 Town, was lured to Bailong Bridge by Liu Changlong, a boat rocker, in July of this year, where he was murdered for his money and his body was abandoned in the Longwangmiao area. After being reported to the Ninth Public Security Bureau, Zhou, the branch chief, arrested the murderer on the spot and sent him to the county government. After interrogation, he confessed his guilt. The county government has sentenced Liu Changlong to death. Once approved, he will be executed in this city.

Outlaw Killed in Tongzhou

Gao Hong, a robber in the city, gathered crowds to rob, but was unsuccessful in his desires. He used vicious methods against the male and female victims to force them to reveal the location of their hidden silver, resulting in many deaths and injuries. The bandit was arrested by the police regiment in the north of the city and was being escorted with a gun when he escaped en route. He was chased and shot by the escorting police, and died from the bullet. The court conducted an inspection on the 17th.

Prosecutor Investigates Girl's Suicide by Jumping into the River

Liu, the chief prosecutor of Nantong County Court, specially summoned people related to the case and Zhang Changchun, the manager of the Zhang Shunji Inn in Tianshenggang, and Tao Huan, a tea servant, to open a court for interrogation, but the cause of death has not yet been determined and investigations will continue in all directions. The case of the Normal School student Fan Xiu, who caused a sensation far and wide, who committed suicide by jumping into the Yangtze River on the Dayu ship.

Three People Injured by Collapsing Wall in Changshu

In front of the Zhou family's house at Qinghejia Bridge inside the Dadongmen, there was a tall wall that had been in disrepair for a long time and was about to collapse. At 4 p.m. on the 17th, two Tao children from across the street were playing under the wall when the wall suddenly collapsed, burying both children. At the time, a Zhou woman was passing by and was also buried. Neighbors heard the noise and came out to rescue the three, who were all barely breathing and unable to move. They were immediately sent to the Jishan Hospital in Beimen for treatment. According to the doctor, the woman's legs were broken, and although both children were seriously injured, their lives could be saved.

Young Woman in Gaoyou Hangs Herself After Being Scolded

In the Dongtouzhakou area of this county, there was a widowed woman surnamed Chou, who was naturally fierce. She had two daughters, one 21 years old and one 8 years old. The Chou woman was very strict with her two daughters. Yesterday, her eldest daughter burned the lunch, which led to her mother scolding her. Overwhelmed with shame and anger, the daughter suddenly had a desire to end her life and hanged herself at night while her family was asleep. When she was discovered this morning, she had already died.

Bandits Attempt to Rob Liuan Gate

At about 8 p.m. the other night, a bandit ship suddenly arrived in Liuanzha Town in this county. More than 20 bandits in the ship, all armed with guns and sticks, landed ashore and attempted to rob. All the shops and residents were extremely panicked and closed their doors. The town's self-defense corps, led by instructor Zheng, went to arrest them, but the bandits immediately returned to the ship and fled towards the center of the lake.

Jingjiang Power Plant Stops Supplying Electricity, Inciting a Strike

The shops and people in the Dongmen city area held a Menglan festival with lanterns for three days, and dragged out various electric lights and reconnected them with temporary lights. When the Jixing Power Plant found out, it cut off the power lines in the area. When the people in the area heard the news, they went to negotiate and wanted the power plant to reconnect the power lines, but the power plant workers refused, which led to a dispute and then violence. The power plant worker Cai Dekui had his clothes torn, and the people Wang Heshang and Wu Donglin were beaten with wooden boards by the power plant workers. A storm then broke out secretly. The power plant stopped supplying electricity that night, and the whole city was dark. The people sent the injured to the county government for examination and all the shops in the lighting area went on strike this morning. They are currently in a stalemate, and it is unknown how to resolve it.

Twelve Salt Vessels Carelessly in Yangzhou

At about 12 p.m. on the 16th, a salt vessel belonging to someone surnamed moored at Shierxu caught fire. Suddenly, the fire was raging. The nearby boaters were awakened from their dreams, and their cries shook the sky. After trying their best to put out the fire, it burned more than a dozen neighboring boats, causing huge losses.

Fire in Hangzhou Kills One

The Luxingquan restaurant at No. 28 Caishiqiao Street in Hangzhou has been open for several years and has had good business. At 1:30 a.m. this morning (18th), due to a careless stove fire, the clouds were filled with thick smoke and could not be approached. The first branch of the Public Security Bureau's seventh resident post urgently telegraphed the Public Security Bureau's fire brigade and the community fire brigade, which dispatched fire trucks to put out the fire. It was extinguished at 2:10 a.m. It is estimated that six houses were burned down at Caishiqiao Street, including Luxingyuan at No. 18, Zhu Shunxing tofu shop at No. 29, Yufenghang grocery store at No. 31, Hair 苍 at No. 46, Huang Chunjie at No. 47, Jinweiji at No. 49 and 50, and Zhang Tangquan at No. 48, a total of 16 houses, with losses of more than 20,000 yuan. Cao Jinlong, a 14-year-old apprentice at the Luxingyuan restaurant, was burned to death in the fire because he could not escape. His head and face were charred, and his limbs were incomplete. His mother rushed to the scene after hearing the news and mourned over his body, which was an extremely tragic sight. The owner of the shop, Xu Xitang, has been detained by the bureau for interrogation.

Lianhua Employee Commits Suicide in Hangzhou

Deng Jiyuan, an employee of the Shanghai Lianhua Film Company, was laid off after the company's former manager died and Wang Yibo took over. He had been unemployed for a long time and was in dire financial straits. He came to Hangzhou from Shanghai a few days ago to visit friends but was unsuccessful. He was staying at No. 7 Xihu Hotel. Last night, he suddenly had a desire to end his life and bought a bottle of ammonia and drank it. He was barely breathing. Fortunately, the tea boy noticed it and reported it to the local police station, and he was rushed to the Municipal Hospital for treatment.

Murder Occurs in Shangyu's Dupu

Shao Baiqing, a resident of the Shantang Village in Dupu, about five li from the Xihaoba Town, is the illegitimate son of the late famous doctor Shao Ji'an. Since Ji'an's death, his brothers have divided the property. Due to the issue of status, he had a dispute with his eldest brother, Zuoqing. Baiqing was addicted to drinking and fighting and colluded with a lawyer surnamed Xia in the city, resulting in endless lawsuits for years. Therefore, his relatives and neighbors hated him to the bone. On the evening of the 8th of this month, Baiqing was drinking at a hotel in Hao and walked home. While drunk, he used an iron rod to smash bowls and plates and left the house resentfully. On the way, he suddenly encountered an assailant who launched a sudden attack. Because of the disparity in numbers and while he was drunk, Baiqing was injured in key parts by a firewood iron hairpin and fell to the ground and died. Subsequently, his half-brother Xiang Ahua and sister reported the injury to the county government on the 10th, and the county government sent personnel to verify it. The corpse's relatives identified the murderer as Shao Mengxiang (ie, Ziqing), the son of Shao Zuoqing, the doctor who committed the crime in the swamp. The accompanying forensic police have taken him to the county for detention.

Deserters Massacre Four Lives in Jiashan

On the night of August 31, four infantrymen (from Anhui) deserted from a certain battalion of the Infantry Fourth Regiment of the Provincial Security Office. Wei Jiehua, the battalion adjutant, led a team to chase them. They traveled through Jiaxing Xincheng and inquired all the way before learning that the deserters had shot and killed four members of the Gu Fulong family, who were reed hut fishermen in the Sitingzi area of Shengze Township, on the night of the 2nd. There were deep bullet wounds on each of them. Three quick-firing rifle bullets, one bead clip, and two bead shells were found next to the bodies. Wang, the chief of the Shengze Public Security Bureau, and Xing Han, the patrol captain, together with the county forensic officer, went to the countryside for inspection. The body of Gu Fulong has not been found anywhere. After this case occurred, the public security agencies in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces paid unusual attention.

Jiashang Cables Request to Abolish Agent Tax for Business Tax

The Jiashan County Chamber of Commerce previously believed that it was harsh to tax buyers via agent collection so they especially cabled the Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce to request a correction. This order has not yet been approved, and the business tax bureau of the third district has already started the investigation and collection. The various agents are in a panic and have come to the Chamber of Commerce to inquire. It is now known that the County Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance on the 17th, asking for immediate correction and to cancel the original plan. It also pushed the chairman of the committee, Shen Xiping, to discuss with the Business Tax Bureau to postpone the investigation and collection.

Local News

Yesterday's Gloomy Wind and Bitter Rain: Solemn Second Anniversary of the (September 18th Incident)

City Flags Flown at Half-Mast and Entertainment Suspended for Mourning

Various Agencies and Organizations Held Commemorative Meetings

Mayor Wu Delivered a Speech Urging People to Work Hard

Yesterday marked the second anniversary of the September 18th Incident. The gloomy wind and bitter rain doubled the sorrow. Throughout the city, flags were flown at half-mast, and entertainment was suspended for mourning. At eleven o'clock in the morning, citizens across the city stopped working and observed five minutes of silence to commemorate the soldiers who sacrificed themselves for the country and the compatriots who were killed. The City Party Headquarters convened representatives from all walks of life at nine o'clock yesterday morning to hold a commemorative meeting. During the City Government's memorial week, Mayor Wu delivered a speech on the efforts that our people should make to commemorate the September 18th Incident. His words were extremely somber and tragic. The authorities of the Chinese and French Concessions took temporary special precautions. The details are recorded as follows:

Representatives from All Walks of Life Attended the Meeting

At nine o'clock yesterday morning, the commemorative meeting convened by the City Party Headquarters with representatives from all walks of life was held in the auditorium on the third floor of the City Party Headquarters. In the center of the venue, a white cloth banner was hung high, reading "Shanghai Representatives from All Walks of Life Hold the (Second Anniversary Commemorative Meeting of the September 18th Incident)." Slogans were posted around the room. The representatives who attended yesterday included Jiang Huaisu, He Yuanming, and Zhou Lianze from the City Party Headquarters; Qiu Yunming and Chen Jixi from the Land Bureau; Li Zemin from the Public Security Bureau; Sheng Yizhang and Zhang Mengling from the Diplomatic Affairs Office; Li Ping and Huang Chongsheng from the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court; Lu Boping from the National Medical Hall; Jiang Guangqian from the University Alliance; Yu Zhenhui from the Municipal Farmers' Association; Zhu Xuefan from the General Labor Union; and representatives from over three hundred organizations and schools such as the Copper and Tin, Sixth District Tea, Fourth District Rubber, Southern Goods, Wood, Military Uniform, Water and Electricity, and Ham trade associations, as well as the Huadong, Huiqiao, Cangji, Songchun, Qinyi, Pengnan, and Huixi schools, and the Party Headquarters of various districts. The meeting ceremony included: (1) Opening the meeting, (2) Singing the Party song, (3) Paying the highest respect to the Party, the national flag, and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (4) Respectfully reading the Prime Minister's will, (5) Observing five minutes of silence to mourn the soldiers who died in the September 18th Incident, (6) Chairman's report, (7) Speeches, (8) Shouting slogans, and (9) Adjournment.

Chairman's Report and Speech Recorded

After the meeting opened and the rituals were performed, Chairman Jiang Huaisu first reported, saying, "Today is the second anniversary of the national humiliation of September 18th. We must know that the remote cause of the September 18th tragedy was entirely due to the Twenty-One Demands, and the immediate cause was the Northeast's construction of the Huludao military port and other issues, which created Japan's attempt to annex North China. I think everyone already understands this. I feel that in this commemoration, we should realize that the occurrence of the September 18th Incident was purely due to the inability of the entire nation to unify its will, which led to numbness, indifference, and a drunken, dreamlike existence, thinking that China is vast and rich in resources, and that no matter who tramples on it, it will not be completely destroyed. The people across the country did not pay much attention to the Wanbaoshan Incident. Although the people of the three northeastern provinces already felt the pain, they did not express any reaction. As for the boycott movement, everyone thought that it would cause unnecessary losses to industry and commerce. It was not until the January 28th Incident that the citizens of Shanghai felt the personal pain of national crisis, and their patriotic emotions became tense. However, the September 18th Incident, because the people across the country failed to resist in unison, resulted in the sacrifice of the four northeastern provinces. We must have the spirit of sacrifice to save the country, and we must have the tools to save the country to save it from danger. As for the tools to save the country, (1) promote knowledge internally, and (2) strengthen military force externally. In the past, people generally despised soldiers. There was a saying that 'good men don't become soldiers.' Now, this concept has been completely broken. We must implement benevolent rule (that is, realize the Three Principles of the People), support small and weak nations, and not rely on the strong to bully the weak. In the January 28th Shanghai Battle, our country used up one-fourth of its bullets, but the war zone was only thirty Chinese miles, which was enough to make the entire nation change color at the mention of it and break their hearts. However, compared with the European War, it was insignificant. This is purely because the people lack military education. From now on, everyone must take this responsibility. There is no need to cry bitterly. We should use our intelligence and work together to save the country. Starting from today, within three years or five years, we will wash away this shame and let the countries of the world know that we are capable and comfort the dead martyrs. Ten years later, we will hold a grand celebration." Next, Cao Peizi from the University Alliance gave a speech, saying, "Just now, the chairman reported that the problem with the people across the country is numbness and indifference. However, Mr. Wang Yunwu once said that the success of education is also a failure, because those who have received higher education cannot do hard labor, which harms the country and the people. I hope that the so-called intellectual class will engage in production and not only seek to be promoted and make a fortune, in order to save the decline." Zhu Xuefan briefly said, "After September 18th, the three northeastern provinces and Rehe fell one after another. The people did not have a unified will, which made it impossible for the government to respond. From now on, we should cooperate with the government to determine the direction and respond to the national crisis. Only then can we live up to the true meaning of commemorating the national crisis."

Slogans and Calls to Defend the Country and Resist Insults

The slogans shouted at the end of the meeting were: (1) September 18th is the greatest day of national humiliation, (2) Continue the spirit of the anti-Japanese martyrs, (3) Save the northeastern disaster victims, (4) Strive to suppress bandits, (5) Develop civil power and strengthen national power, (6) Recover the lost territories in the Northeast, (7) Down with Japanese imperialism, (8) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang, (9) Long live the Republic of China. There were also many slogans on the walls, excerpts from which are as follows: (1) Seek to wipe out the shame and avenge through developing production and strengthening national power, (2) Abandon civil wars, unify will, and work together to appease the country and resist foreign aggression, (3) Suppressing the Red bandits is an essential task for appeasing the country and resisting foreign aggression, (4) Commemorating the national crisis of September 18th, we should strive to develop the Northwest and consolidate the national borders, (5) The September 18th Incident is the greatest day of national humiliation when the Japanese pirates occupied the Northeast, (6) Inherit the spirit of sacrifice of the anti-Japanese martyrs in defending the country and resisting insults.

Mayor's Speech Was Somber and Tragic

The Municipal Government held a joint commemoration of the September 18th Incident during the Prime Minister's Memorial Week yesterday morning. Mayor Wu led the heads of various bureaus and all colleagues of the Municipal Government to stand and observe five minutes of silence to express their deep condolences to the soldiers who sacrificed themselves for the country in the battles of the three northeastern provinces, Rehe, Luandong, and the Great Wall. Mayor Wu also delivered a speech entitled "The Efforts That the People Should Make to Commemorate the September 18th Incident" to inspire the people. The text of Mayor Wu's speech is recorded as follows: "Comrades, today is the Prime Minister's Memorial Week, and it coincides with the commemoration of September 18th. Today, the people of Shanghai should feel particularly sad about commemorating September 18th compared to the people in other places, because during the January 28th Incident, they all experienced it firsthand and deeply felt the pain of the national crisis. They recognized the danger of the national crisis. Therefore, today, when commemorating September 18th, their sorrowful emotions are of course even greater than those of people in other places. However, have the people across the country been commemorating September 18th year after year by holding a commemorative meeting, saying a few sad words, or writing a few articles to publish in the newspaper, and thinking that they have done their best to commemorate it? I remember Mr. Wu Zhihui once said that during the Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu, the people across the country were all shouting and crying for saving the country. Shouting and crying for saving the country is, of course, a sincere and enthusiastic expression of the patriotic emotions of the people across the country, but from the year of Jiawu to now, decades have passed. During these decades, because the people across the country only shouted and cried but did not work hard to engage in the movement to save the country and the actual work of saving the country, the country has not only not been saved today but has instead added several layers of national crisis, and the national situation is becoming increasingly dangerous. Also, according to a friend, Mr. Ma Xiangbo once said that he fled the country on the day he was born, and he is still fleeing today. Mr. Ma is now ninety-four years old. The time he was born was just the time of the Opium War. It has been nearly a century since then. It can be seen that the national crisis of our China has had such a long history. This is not because the people across the country do not know how to save the country, but they do not know how to do the work of saving the country from a practical point of view. Therefore, from decades ago until now, they are still only shouting and crying. But we must know that this kind of erroneous national psychology is even more dangerous than knocking on the door and pressing the territory. If we do not correct it in time, our country and nation will inevitably send him his final resting place in the near future. Therefore, today, when commemorating September 18th, we should not just hold a commemorative meeting to talk about a few words or write a few articles to publish and think that it is over. Instead, the people across the country must make a great determination and do it practically. I believe that if we do the work of saving the country in this way, we will definitely have considerable room for improvement. The Prime Minister said that the biggest problem with the Chinese people is relying on heaven for food. Our country has become weak to this point today because of this problem of relying on heaven for food. Of course, the nations of the world have all gone through the theocratic era. In the heyday of theocracy, all countries, like China, entrusted their own destiny to the unknown (number) by seeking gods and divination and completely wiped out all their own abilities. However, the period of time that we Chinese people have relied on heaven for food is particularly long compared to all the countries in the world. Even today, we are still relying on heaven for food. Therefore, like last year's military disasters and man-made disasters in the Yangtze River, the serious national disasters that were intertwined and overwhelmed were all attributed to numbers, thinking that they were not something that human power could resist, and not admitting that they had the ability and knowledge to save the current national crisis.

National Revival Through Hardship and Struggle

However, we do not know that the current national crisis is not a (number) entirely caused by our people, and that everything should be attributed to people. All current difficulties and any problems can be saved and resolved from our personnel affairs. Therefore, during this period of national crisis, the people across the country should understand the reasons for causing the national crisis, and at the same time, they must recognize how we can save the country so that the country can be saved, and how we can save the country so that the national crisis can be resolved. If we recognize the great way to save the country, the people across the country must make a great determination and always remember that if we do not work hard, the country will perish, and if we do not work hard, we will have nothing to eat. We must work hard towards this great way. The ancients said, "(National revival through hardship)" and "(A country that has no enemies abroad will always perish)." Now is the most difficult time for China. The people across the country should wake up together and correct all the past erroneous psychologies in order to save the country from its current crisis. We see that in ancient and modern times, both at home and abroad, whether it is a country or an individual, the success of their careers has always come from the most difficult and arduous circumstances. Our Chinese nation has reached the most difficult and arduous period in its history today, the twenty-second year of the Republic of China. From now on, the people across the country should unite and engage in the main plan for saving the country at present, namely national defense construction and economic construction. National defense construction is used to resist foreign aggression and save the country from danger. Economic construction is used to revive the bankrupt rural areas and relieve the hunger of the people. National defense construction and economic construction must also go hand in hand. If you want to achieve success in national defense construction, you must implement economic construction. If you want to achieve success in economic construction, you must also implement national defense construction. If the people across the country can base themselves on this plan to save the country and work hard from a practical point of view, China will definitely be able to achieve the ultimate success of adversity turning into prosperity in the future. Today, I would like to encourage my compatriots across the country with this idea, and I also encourage myself."

The meeting was presided over by Zhang Xiang, the acting commander and chief of staff. Finally, the chairman gave a speech on the meaning and responsibility of commemorating the September 18th Incident. The speech was passionate and inspiring, and all the soldiers in the audience were filled with grief and anger, sharing a common hatred of the enemy. The meeting adjourned at around 12:00 noon. In addition, the Special Party Headquarters of the Municipal Security Bureau convened representatives of officers and soldiers of various teams and staff members of the association, about 200 people in total, to hold a commemorative meeting at 11:00 a.m. yesterday. Li Jingcong of Eurasia Company Will Test-Fly to Qinghai This Morning

Chairman of Qinghai Province Ma Lin Sends a Telegram to Welcome Him

Will First Go to Dihua and Tacheng in Xinjiang and Then Fly to Qinghai

In order to prepare for the opening of the air route from Lanzhou, Gansu to Xining, the provincial capital of Qinghai, Li Jingcong, the general manager of the Eurasia Aviation Company, had originally planned to depart for a test flight at the end of last month. However, because Li went to Ping to visit his sick mother, he was unable to do so. It is now known that the various preparations have been completed, and it has been decided to depart from the Hongqiao Airport at 6:00 a.m. today (the 19th). In addition to Li himself, only one pilot and one radio operator will accompany him. It is reported that this trip will follow the northwest route to Xinjiang, Dihua, Tacheng, and other places for inspection. When he returns to Lanzhou, he will transfer to Xining, Qinghai. Ma Lin, the chairman of the Qinghai Provincial Government, has already sent a telegram to welcome him.

Japanese Envoy Arima's Remarks

Stating that the Sino-Japanese Issue

Will Begin Negotiations

The Mainland Daily reported that Japanese Minister Akira Arita met with journalists at the Japanese Consulate General yesterday, summarizing his trip to Beijing. He said that, according to his speculation, negotiations between China and Japan would begin in the near future. Arita claimed that his stay in Beijing for one day was only to meet Wang Jingwei, who was also acting as the Minister of Foreign Affairs. The discussion on diplomatic issues was quite smooth. In addition, he verified the rumor that Chiang Tso-pin, the ambassador to Japan, would return to his post in Tokyo, saying that General Chiang would return to Beijing from Guling on Saturday and would come to Shanghai within a day or two to prepare to go to Japan. Regarding the situation in North China, Arita said that the important issues in the north had been resolved, and General Huang Fu would return to the north within a few days. When asked by reporters whether he would return to his country for a trip, Arita replied that he had not yet received orders from Tokyo. He also expressed surprise at the change of the Japanese Foreign Minister, saying that he had not heard of it beforehand and only learned of it after returning to Shanghai yesterday.

Page 10

The Second Hurricane Hit Shanghai Last Night

The Wind Was More Violent Than the Last Time

North-South Ocean and Shanghai-Ningbo Ships Were All Suspended Yesterday

Tidal Inversion Caused Flooding of Low-Lying Roads

The second hurricane, in two phases, with one currently moving slowly north from the southeast of Taiwan, and the other having reached the sea off the Zhoushan Islands at 9:00 p.m. last night, entering Hangzhou Bay, hit Shanghai last night. The Customs House has notified all ships to postpone their departure to avoid accidents. The weather was dark yesterday, with strong winds and heavy rain, continuing throughout the day, and even worse in the afternoon. In the evening, the tide of the Huangpu River was agitated by the hurricane and flowed backwards, causing flooding of low-lying roads in the concession, with water depths reaching the shins or knees, a very serious situation. As of 3:00 a.m. this morning, the water began to recede. The details are recorded below:

Passed Hangzhou Bay Yesterday

The local observatory issued its first report at 11:00 a.m. yesterday, stating that the hurricane was sailing in the East China Sea, having reached 27 degrees 30 minutes north latitude and 123 degrees east longitude at 10:00 a.m., moving northwest towards the coast of Zhejiang and tilting further north, possibly passing over Shanghai at night. At the same time, Shanghai would experience a flood at midnight. Later, at 5:00 p.m., a second report was issued, stating that the hurricane had reached the coast between Wenzhou and Ningbo in Zhejiang, moving northwest by north, at 28 and a half degrees north latitude and 121 and a half degrees east longitude at 2:00 p.m. (according to which the location is on the coast of Wenzhou Bay). The center of the hurricane was 60 miles away. The wind would tilt further north-northwest and would pass over western Shanghai at night, with strong winds and rain and a lighter sea tide. At 9:30 p.m., the New Sound Society reporter obtained the observatory's final report, learning that the wind had changed direction at 9:00 p.m. last night, reaching 30 miles east of Ningbo, at 30 degrees north latitude and 122 degrees east longitude, when the Hangzhou Bay and Zhoushan Islands area was only 90 miles away from Shanghai. The wind was very violent and is now turning directly north. From the current situation, it will pass over Shanghai at around 1:00 a.m. this morning.

A Study of the Hurricane's Course

The course of this hurricane is quite strange. When it departed from the ocean west-northwest of Guam, an American territory, at 16 degrees north latitude and 136 degrees east longitude on the 11th of this month, it was heading directly for the East China Sea. On the 12th of this month, it suddenly changed direction and circled in a circle between 18 and 21 degrees latitude and 126 and 128 and a half degrees longitude from the 13th to the 15th. On the 16th of this month, it returned to 20 degrees north latitude and 125 and a half degrees east longitude and turned northwest. At 6:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, it reached the southeast of Wen County, on the ocean at 25 degrees north latitude and 124 degrees east longitude. Yesterday morning, it reached a point more than 120 miles east of Wenzhou. At 2:00 p.m., it advanced further to the shore of Wenzhou Bay. However, hurricanes that circle during the journey have only occurred twice last year, and this is the first time this year.

The Wind Was More Violent Than Before

According to the Westerners at the observatory, this hurricane was more violent than the last one. When the last hurricane passed through the area north of Huanao Mountain, the wind force in this city was 10. However, Shanghai is only more than 80 miles away from Huanao Mountain. This hurricane reached 27 and a half degrees north latitude, which is 123 degrees east longitude and outside Wenzhou, at 6:00 a.m. yesterday, and already had a wind force of 10. This proves that the wind force was more violent than before. This city had a wind force of 4 yesterday morning, which increased to 6 in the afternoon, and 8 at 9:00 p.m. last night. Huanao Mountain had a wind force of 10.

The Jianghai Customs Fired a Cannon

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 p.m., the Customs House received a notice from the observatory that a hurricane was approaching Shanghai and immediately fired a wind warning cannon and hung a large black ball on the roof of the building. A very large black ball was also hung high on the Meteorological Observatory on the Bund of Edward Road to indicate that a hurricane was approaching Shanghai.

The Institute of Research Reports

A Central News Agency report on the 18th stated that the Meteorological Research Institute of the Academia Sinica reported on the 18th that this hurricane was discovered in the ocean northeast of Luzon four or five days ago. It initially moved northwest, passed east of Taiwan on the 17th, and entered the East China Sea at 6:00 a.m. on the 18th. It continued to move northwest and approached the vicinity of Wenzhou at 2:00 p.m., and will likely land at Yong at night. The coastal areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang will likely suffer more damage from the storm than the last hurricane.

Zhejiang Sea Ships Suspended

The local Ningbo, Shanghai-Taiwan, Wenzhou, and Ruiping liners were still preparing to depart at 12:00 noon yesterday. Therefore, ships such as the Xinning, Shaoxing, and Xin Beijing still boarded passengers. After receiving the Customs House's warning cannon in the afternoon, it was decided to suspend navigation and refund tickets to all passengers who had boarded the ship, asking them to disembark and leave tomorrow (Wednesday). The Wenzhou and Taiwan ships also stopped sailing. All Shanghai-Zhejiang sea ships were stopped yesterday. At the same time, an urgent telegram was sent to Ningbo, instructing ships such as the Ningxing and Xinjiangtian to also not come. Therefore, no Ningbo ships will arrive today either.

Exporting Liner Postponement

This morning, North and South Pacific liners exporting from Shanghai, including the Taikoo's "Suzhou," "Xinjiang," and "Shengjing," Jardine Matheson's "Jiesheng" and "Lisheng," the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Taishun," and the Dalian Steamship Company's "Dalian No. 9," among others, were all prevented from loading cargo due to severe wind and rain yesterday afternoon. At 4:00 PM, a hurricane warning was issued. Therefore, the companies notified the ocean liners to postpone the departure of the aforementioned ships. They will depart after the hurricane passes. Ships en route that are unable to reach Shanghai were also ordered to anchor offshore to avoid the storm and prevent accidents.

Huangpu River Tidal Inversion

From 8:00 PM last night, fierce winds and torrential rain struck the city, with a force no less than the previous hurricane. The wind strengthened the waves, and the waves amplified the wind's power, creating a scene of ten thousand horses galloping and surging on the Huangpu River. Low-lying areas were flooded. The following is a record of the water situation in various places around midnight last night:

Songhu Railway Interruption

Zhanghuabang, located near the coast, along with Paotaiwan, is a town near the mouth of the Wusong River. The embankment there is built with huge stones and is quite sturdy. However, due to years of disrepair, it has eroded considerably. The last time a major typhoon passed through, it almost caused a major disaster. Local authorities are currently working hard to repair it. Unexpectedly, it was hit by wind and waves again last night. There is no report as of the time the reporter is filing this article. However, it is understood that the water level is rising relentlessly. Around 8:00 PM, it was level with the shore. Around 9:00 PM, it surged onto the railway tracks, only a foot or so below the station platform, making the situation very dangerous. Therefore, the Songhu train could not proceed and only went as far as Zhanghuabang Station. Around 12:00 AM, Zhanghuabang Station and the Zhanghuabang Railway Factory were also flooded. Consequently, the Songhu train was blocked again after reaching the Wusong branch station and had to turn back. It is reported that the water level is still rising rapidly, and the situation is very serious. As traffic to Wusong is completely cut off, the true situation is unclear. However, judging from the turbulent waters, the seawall is unlikely to be in good condition.

Flooded Roads

In the International Settlement, Nanjing Road (Yinghua Street) and the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Nanjing Road, as well as low-lying roads such as Beijing Road (Guizhou Road), were flooded around 10:00 PM. By 11:00 PM, the water had risen more than a foot. Nanjing Road, Jiujiang Road, Hankou Road, Fuzhou Road, Guangdong Road, and the Bund were subsequently flooded, and the flooding gradually expanded. Soon, Henan Road and Shandong Road were also affected. Around 12:00 AM, the water level in front of this newspaper's office had reached more than a foot, and in front of the Central Police Station, it was nearly three feet. Even rickshaws had difficulty passing through, and automobiles were completely disabled, with some breaking down in the middle of the road. By 12:30 AM, all the shops in the Zhoujinli area were flooded. Coupled with the howling wind, the water level continued to rise. There were no pedestrians on the streets, and even rickshaws had disappeared. Occasionally, one or two were waiting for hire on the road, but only for exorbitant prices.

Suffering of the Poor in Zhabei

In Zhabei and the Nanshi area, countless shanties of the poor were blown down by the wind. As a result, these poor people were emaciated and sought shelter under the eaves of various lanes or houses. Furthermore, with successive huge waves, they invaded various places, suddenly losing their homes. They ran around to escape, in a very miserable state. Therefore, last night, the entire city of Shanghai was almost entirely in a state of wind and rain, and the situation was very critical.

Emergency Repair of the Wusong Seawall

Yesterday morning, the wind and rain at the mouth of the Wusong River were fierce, and the tide rose sharply. At its highest point, it was only five or six inches from the top of the seawall. Nearby residents were greatly alarmed. However, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works had not yet sent anyone to help. Therefore, Tang Chengzhong, a member of the Wusong Municipal Council, temporarily purchased hundreds of sacks, hired more than eighty workers, and sent them along with staff to the seawall in the Wumufeng area to repair the breaches and prevent any accidents. Committee Member Tang rushed to Shanghai at 9:00 AM yesterday to urge the Bureau of Public Works. This reporter braved the rain in the afternoon and went to the seawall to investigate the dangerous situation. He saw that the soil inside the stone embankment in the Wumufeng area had also loosened and subsided. Mr. Liu, the supervisor sent by the Municipal Committee Office, told this reporter that this section had been severely damaged and that the project was quite large. At the moment, it is being repeatedly ravaged by wind and rain, so only the breaches can be repaired first, and the major project will be officially repaired by the Bureau of Public Works, and so on. This reporter left Wusong around 4:00 PM and saw several trucks from the Bureau of Public Works coming from Waitan, fully loaded with workers, heading towards Paotaiwan.

Baoshan County Patrols the Embankments

Jin Qingzhang, Bao Siren, and Wan Kaijia of the Baoshan County Government have strictly ordered the embankment patrolmen to take strict precautions. Zhu Kaichou and Hong Jingping, gentry from Taicang, are also contacting local public organizations.

Another Hurricane

According to reports, another hurricane was located in the sea southeast of Taiwan. At 6:00 AM yesterday, it was at 22.5 degrees north latitude and 121.5 degrees east longitude, heading due north. At 2:00 PM, it had moved to 23 degrees north latitude and 123 degrees east longitude, still heading due north.

The "Ta Mei Wan Bao" Reports

Today (the 18th), the strong winds and heavy rains in the city are a precursor to another hurricane strike. This is the twenty-first hurricane of the year. It originated west of Guam on the 11th of this month and initially moved westward. After several hundred miles, it turned northwest, changing its direction in the sea northeast of northern Luzon. It is heading directly towards the Zhejiang coast and is expected to reach the area between Wenzhou and Ningbo this afternoon. After making landfall, it may pass west of Shanghai, sparing the city from a direct hit. However, in any case, the hurricane rains in the city will intensify tonight and tomorrow morning. According to news from Wenzhou, the wind force there is ten units. Furthermore, around 6:00 AM this morning, the wind force at the Daxie Island, outside the mouth of the Yangtze River, had reached six units, and there was a growing trend of intensifying. In addition, there is another hurricane, the twenty-second of the year, originating near Taiwan and heading north, closely following the first hurricane. The wind force is also quite strong, but slightly less than the first hurricane.

The "Ta Mei Wan Bao" reports, according to reliable sources, the National Government has signed a contract with an American aircraft company to deliver fifteen new-style Curtiss Hawk II aircraft as soon as possible, with the Hangzhou airfield as the base. New Regulations for Export of Merchant Vessels Starting October 1st

Seafarers Do Not Receive Navigation Bureau Manuals

Customs Implements Ban on Clearance

Navigation Bureau Increases Substantial Revenue

The Shanghai Navigation Bureau has been rigorously registering all crew members of ships, and has issued a final notice to the ship companies. If the crew members do not register and pay fees at the bureau to receive manuals, even if they have certificates from the Ministry, it has been agreed with the Customs to ban the ship from clearance and prohibit its export. This matter is of great importance, and the following investigation and report is made:

Registration Manual

The Shanghai Navigation Bureau stipulates that all deck and engine crew members on ships, even if they have already received certificates from the Ministry of Transportation, must still register at the Navigation Bureau and receive their crew manuals. A fee must be paid when receiving the manual: 4 yuan for shipowners, 3 yuan for chief and second officers, 3 yuan for chief engineer, and 3 yuan for first and second assistant engineers. Seamen pay 1 yuan each. Unemployed seamen must also register and receive a reduction of 2 yuan. Ships are not allowed to employ anyone who does not register and receive this manual. Because there are not many people going to receive them, a stern notice has been issued, with a deadline of the end of this month. Otherwise, the merchant ships will be detained.

Prohibition of Clearance

Yesterday, in order to rigorously implement the registration of navigation manuals, the Navigation Bureau specially requested and was approved by the Ministry of Transportation to inform the Jianghai Customs that the Navigation Bureau had newly created a single form for the export of merchant vessels. From October 1st, ships will not be allowed to depart without this export form. The names, native places, and Ministry certificate numbers of the crew members must be clearly filled in on this export form, along with the registration numbers from the Navigation Bureau manual. The form must be submitted to the Customs for inspection when the ship departs, and clearance will be granted based on this form. If there is no export form, or if the crew members on the form have not received the Navigation Bureau manual, clearance will be strictly prohibited, starting October 1st.

Shipping Bureaus Urge Action

Yesterday, the shipping bureaus received notice of this export form. Since the export of ships cannot be delayed, if any crew members have not gone to the Navigation Bureau to pay the fee and obtain the certificate, then the merchant ship will suffer a significant loss when it is banned from clearance at the time. Therefore, yesterday, the shipping bureaus notified the shipowners, chief officers, second officers, chief engineers, and first and second assistant engineers of all merchant ships, ordering them to quickly go to the Navigation Bureau to pay the fee and buy the manual by September 30th, when the ship arrives in Shanghai. Otherwise, in order to protect the ship's operations and avoid being banned from clearance, the shipping company will have to replace the unregistered crew members with crew members who have the manual.

Yesterday, the Japanese-language "Shanghai Daily" reported that the newly appointed commander of the Third Fleet, Lieutenant General Imamura, is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 3:00 PM tomorrow aboard his flagship Izumo. Page 11

Robbery Case on Rue Paul Beau: Car Still Not Found

Victim Shen Yangsheng's Whereabouts Unknown

Suspect Arrested and Interrogated

Zhao Liansheng, also known as Xiao Liansheng, a Ningbo native residing at No. 10 Pubo Lane on Rue Paul Beau in the French Concession, accompanied his wife, Cao, and friend, Shen Yangsheng, to the Jia family in Sande Lane across the street at 8:45 AM the day before yesterday to pay respects. The three walked together to the intersection of Rue Paul Beau and Rue Luban and boarded their private car. As they approached the car, they encountered bandits who attempted to kidnap them. Zhao cleverly drew his self-defense pistol and fired to defend himself, managing to escape. However, his friend, Shen Yangsheng, was forced into the car, and the driver, Zhu Wenyu, was ordered to drive away. The police arrived at the scene, arrested one bandit, Gu Junshan, confiscated a pistol and eleven bullets, and took him to the police station for investigation. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday at noon, the police sent the arrested bandit Gu Jinshan, along with the pistol and bullets, to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District, where Judge Li Changnian interrogated him. Fei Xizhen, the police lawyer, stated the case, saying that the defendant, along with several accomplices, attempted to kidnap Zhao Liansheng on Rue Paul Beau yesterday but failed. The police chased and arrested the defendant, but the victim's friend, surnamed Shen, and the driver and car have been taken away and their whereabouts are still unknown. As the police have not yet investigated the case, he requested that the defendant be detained and the hearing postponed for two weeks for a detailed investigation and the arrest of accomplices. He also presented the pistol and bullets as evidence. The defendant, Gu Junshan, 27 years old, from Funing, said that he used to be a rickshaw puller and had been a soldier, but now he is unemployed and has no residence, borrowing a place to stay with relatives near the Longhua headquarters. He said that the pistol in the case was his, but he had not fired it. The court verified the statement and ordered the hearing to be postponed to October 5th, and the defendant was taken back into custody.

It is further reported that since the incident occurred, the French police have been doing their best to investigate and have also notified the police stations in the Public Concession and the districts of Nanshi and Zhabei under the jurisdiction of the Chinese Public Security Bureau to pay attention to intercepting Zhao's stolen car and Zhao's kidnapped friend, Shen Yangsheng, and the driver, Wei Wenyu. However, as of last night, Zhao's car had not been found. The French police believe that no matter how late, Zhao's car would definitely be found by this morning at the latest. Unexpectedly, as of last night, the car had still not been found, which is unprecedented in the history of robbery cases. In the past, whenever a robbery case occurred in Shanghai, the car stolen by the robbers would be found within a few hours at most. This time, the car has been missing for nearly two days and one night, and there is still no trace of it, so the police are deeply surprised. However, the French police predict that if there is still no new development by today, the robbers will definitely drive the car out of Shanghai, or drive to Hangzhou along the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. It is also possible that the robbers are cunning and may have destroyed the evidence, or even sunk the car in the ocean or the Huangpu River, which is also a possibility. As for the robbers temporarily hiding the car to wait for the future, even if the robbers are stupid, they would probably not be so foolish.

Fee Schedule for Building Plans Set by the French Municipal Council

The French Municipal Council of Shanghai has stipulated the fee schedule for the map fees for building permits requested by various construction companies, so that the builders can attach the map to the application form for the building permit. The rules are as follows: (A) Land that has already been surveyed: (1) For land under six mu, contained in one land register number, the fee is five taels of silver per map. (2) For land above six mu, contained in one land register number, the fee is ten taels of silver per map. (3) For land with multiple land register numbers, the fee will be doubled according to the previous item. (B) Land that has not been surveyed: (1) Land under two mu, the fee is ten taels of silver per map. (2) Land under two mu, the fee is fifteen taels of silver per map. (3) Land under five mu, the fee is twenty taels of silver per map. (4) For land above five mu, for each additional mu, the fee will increase by two taels of silver per map. The above fee schedule is only applicable to building permit applications. All measurement fees and land register map fees determined by the Board of Directors on December 17, 1931, will still be implemented as before. (C) However, in order to allow builders to store the building map and the building attachments for record purposes, the Bureau may, at the time of applying for the building permit, approve the application of the relevant person and issue additional maps according to the following prices: (1) For land of six mu or less, one tael of silver per attached map. (2) For land above six mu, two taels of silver per map.
